msg:When you come to Tianjin to take the test, the best hotel near the test room is Hyatt. Take the high-speed rail to Tianjin, directly transfer to Metro Line 2 for 3 stops, and walk for 5 minutes. It is very convenient to choose public transportation.
I got a room on the 16th floor. The front desk staff was also very nice and had a good attitude. The floor-to-ceiling windows of the room had a good view and the room was very clean. There is a 24-hour small supermarket on the first floor of the hotel. Although the price is slightly higher, it can be considered as a complete product if it is an emergency.
I went to the gym to practice the ellipse for a while at night. It is recommended to bring bottled water in the room. The gym seems to only have water from a drinking fountain. The gym is not big, facing the swimming pool, and there are a lot of people swimming on weekends.
Overall it is good and recommend staying.
